                 <h3 class="Mb(4px) Mb(0px)--md1160 LineClamp(2,42px) Lh(21px)"> <a href="https://www.yahoo.com/news/satan-2-putin-tells-u-121319520.html" class="O(n):f C($m_blue):f D(b)  js-stream-content-link js-stream-item-title js-content-title C($link) C($m_blue):h Td(n) Fz(17px) Fw(b)" data-ylk="cpos:2;cposy:7;bpos:1;pos:1;ss_cid:17f65804-87a9-48b7-a378-a24a15c2d2ee;refcnt:2;subsec:362;imgt:ss;g:bcbe009d-ffb5-3f93-b9b5-dbd9211ea643;ct:1;pkgt:cluster_all_img;grpt:storyCluster;cnt_tpc:World;elm:hdln;elmt:ct;r:40000270005S00001;ccode:mdsfb;"><span>Satan 2: Putin Tells U.S. 'You Will Listen To Russia Now' as he Deploys Hypersonic Nuclear ICBM</span><u class="Pos(a) T(0) Start(0) W(100%) H(100%) strm-stretch"></u></a> </h3> 
                 <div> 
                  <p class=" stream-summary LineClamp(2,34px) Lh(17px) C($gray) Bfv(h) D(n)--md1160">Russian&nbsp;President Vladimir Putin said Russia is developing a new generation of advanced nuclear weapons including a hypersonic intercontinental ballistic missile (ICBM) that can reach almost anywhere in the world and cannot be shot down by anti-missile systems. Putin made the claim during his annual presidential address to the Federal Assembly in Moscow. Putin said other countries only listen to Russia when it creates new weapons systems, reported Sputnik, another of Russia’s state organs.&nbsp;“You will listen to us now,” he added.</p> 
                 </div>

                 <h3 class="Mb(4px) Mb(0px)--md1160 LineClamp(2,42px) Lh(21px)"> <a href="https://www.yahoo.com/gma/concealed-carry-permit-holder-flips-script-shoots-kills-162203257--abc-news-topstories.html" class="O(n):f C($m_blue):f D(b)  js-stream-content-link js-stream-item-title js-content-title C($link) C($m_blue):h Td(n) Fz(17px) Fw(b)" data-ylk="cpos:4;cposy:13;bpos:1;pos:1;ss_cid:3e209f7d-bd14-4207-a6ac-d31c67e654bc;refcnt:2;subsec:3753;imgt:ss;g:cb55d1cc-faa0-3431-8e2f-ee7f2e874879;ct:1;pkgt:cluster_all_img;grpt:storyCluster;cnt_tpc:U.S.;elm:hdln;elmt:ct;r:40000271906S00001;ccode:mdsfb;"><span>Concealed-carry permit holder flips the script, shoots and kills alleged carjacker</span><u class="Pos(a) T(0) Start(0) W(100%) H(100%) strm-stretch"></u></a> </h3> 
                 <div> 
                  <p class=" stream-summary LineClamp(2,34px) Lh(17px) C($gray) Bfv(h) D(n)--md1160">A Wisconsin man, using a gun licensed under a concealed-carry permit, shot and killed an alleged carjacker in his company’s parking lot, a city official said. The unidentified employee, 24, had just arrived for work at Milwaukee Machine Tool Corp., shortly before 6 a.m. Monday when a man named Carlos Martin, 21, allegedly attempted to carjack him with a gun, Milwaukee city alderman Cavalier Johnson told ABC News. The Machine Tool worker had a concealed-carry permit, Johnson said, and used his legal weapon to shoot Martin, who died from his injuries.</p>

                 <h3 class="Mb(4px) Mb(0px)--md1160 LineClamp(2,42px) Lh(21px)"> <a href="https://sports.yahoo.com/twitter-goes-wild-james-harden-044808721.html" class="O(n):f C($m_blue):f D(b)  js-stream-content-link js-stream-item-title js-content-title C($link) C($m_blue):h Td(n) Fz(17px) Fw(b)" data-ylk="cpos:6;cposy:17;bpos:1;pos:1;ss_cid:0ead05ff-50e0-4eb9-92ee-641f7b642a80;refcnt:2;subsec:124;imgt:ss;g:62fc024e-66b5-3bb6-9fd9-1e7cd23b43ee;ct:1;pkgt:cluster_all_img;grpt:storyCluster;cnt_tpc:Sports;elm:hdln;elmt:ct;r:40000264131S00001;ccode:mdsfb;"><span>Twitter Goes Wild After James Harden Puts Wesley Johnson on His Knees, Waits to Hit Step-Back Three</span><u class="Pos(a) T(0) Start(0) W(100%) H(100%) strm-stretch"></u></a> </h3> 
                 <div> 
                  <p class=" stream-summary LineClamp(2,34px) Lh(17px) C($gray) Bfv(h) D(n)--md1160">James Harden's game tends to divide NBA fans on Twitter at times, but Wednesday night, all were in agreement that The Beard took disrespect to another level when crossed over Wesley Johnson and made him fall, before stepping back and taking his time to knock down an uncontested three-pointer.The Harden crossover that makes a defender look silly is something we have all seen before. The Harden step-back three that tends to follow said crossover, is also a staple of the six-time All-Star's game that we are all accustomed to watching go in with regularity.But this play entered another stratosphere in the realm of Harden highlights thanks to the pause he takes before releasing his shot. Harden gives Johnson a chance to stand and the rest of the Clippers the opportunity to contest his shot, but when the entire court stood still, he launched up a three and sent the Rockets' bench (make sure you watch Trevor Ariza running up the sideline all the way to half court) and Twitter into a frenzy.The Beard and the Rockets have been having their way so far in their first game against the Clippers and first game in Los Angeles since reportedly using a back tunnel to get into the Clippers' locker room after a 113-102 loss last month.Harden had 22 points in the first half to help Houston build a 61-43 advantage.</p>

                 <h3 class="Mb(4px) Mb(0px)--md1160 LineClamp(2,42px) Lh(21px)"> <a href="https://www.yahoo.com/finance/m/b50cf9b9-e5e0-32e2-8d4f-2c48d208d90e/ss_%E2%80%98american-chopper%E2%80%99-star-sued.html" data-share-link="https://pagesix.com/2018/02/28/american-chopper-star-sued-for-fraud/" class="O(n):f C($m_blue):f D(b)  js-stream-content-link js-stream-item-title js-content-title C($link) C($m_blue):h Td(n) Fz(17px) Fw(b)" data-ylk="cpos:11;cposy:30;bpos:1;pos:1;ss_cid:0bd1e0ab-6f98-4eec-b31b-39cb4efba052;refcnt:2;subsec:0;imgt:ss;g:b50cf9b9-e5e0-32e2-8d4f-2c48d208d90e;ct:1;pkgt:cluster_all_img;grpt:storyCluster;cnt_tpc:Business;elm:hdln;elmt:ct;r:4000026633S00008;ccode:mdsfb;" rel="nofollow" data-attrcat="news"><span>‘American Chopper’ star sued for fraud</span><u class="Pos(a) T(0) Start(0) W(100%) H(100%) strm-stretch"></u></a> </h3> 
                 <div> 
                  <p class=" stream-summary LineClamp(2,34px) Lh(17px) C($gray) Bfv(h) D(n)--md1160">“American Chopper” star Paul Teutul Sr. is being sued for allegedly sabotaging a TV project and costing his business partner millions of dollars. Page Six obtained the Delaware State Chancery Court documents filed in April, which claim that Teutul used Thomas Derbyshire’s investment in an “American Chopper” reboot to fund his personal expenses. Derbyshire said that he agreed to work with Teutul on the show “Orange County Choppers: American Made” for A&amp;E in 2015, but their business agreement quickly went south after Teutul tried to change their 51/49 percent ownership deal (benefiting Derbyshire) to a 50/50 deal. Derbyshire had agreed to fund the project up to $3 million at that time. He claimed</p>

                 <h3 class="Mb(4px) Mb(0px)--md1160 LineClamp(2,42px) Lh(21px)"> <a href="https://www.yahoo.com/gma/missing-cdc-employee-last-fall-said-trying-help-232258916--abc-news-topstories.html" class="O(n):f C($m_blue):f D(b)  js-stream-content-link js-stream-item-title js-content-title C($link) C($m_blue):h Td(n) Fz(17px) Fw(b)" data-ylk="cpos:14;cposy:39;bpos:1;pos:1;ss_cid:52ae87ca-9968-492b-84be-234604e1f1d5;refcnt:2;subsec:98;imgt:ss;g:53620b6b-17b7-3129-a44f-9da2bd0b8f3a;ct:1;pkgt:cluster_all_img;grpt:storyCluster;cnt_tpc:Health;elm:hdln;elmt:ct;r:4000083528S00001;ccode:mdsfb;"><span>Missing CDC employee last fall said he was trying to 'help the lives of others'</span><u class="Pos(a) T(0) Start(0) W(100%) H(100%) strm-stretch"></u></a> </h3> 
                 <div> 
                  <p class=" stream-summary LineClamp(2,34px) Lh(17px) C($gray) Bfv(h) D(n)--md1160">Months before Centers for Disease Control and Prevention employee Timothy Cunningham disappeared, he had been named one of the Atlanta Business Chronicle's 40 Under 40 for 2017 -- a group of young leaders who succeed in their professions and lead their communities, according to the newspaper. &quot;I am using the skills I have to improve and help the lives of others,&quot; Cunningham told the Atlanta Business Chronicle in November. Cunningham, 35, a commander in the Public Health Service who has been sent to respond to public health emergencies including the Ebola virus and the Zika virus, hasn't been seen since Feb. 12.</p>

                    function patchLangBundlesRequires(Y, loader) {
                        var getRequires = loader.getRequires;
                        loader.getRequires = function (mod) {
                            var i, j, m, name, mods, loadDefaultBundle,
                                locales = Y.config.lang || [],
                                r = getRequires.apply(this, arguments);
                            // expanding requirements with optional requires
                            if (mod.langBundles && !mod.langBundlesExpanded) {
                                mod.langBundlesExpanded = [];
                                locales = typeof locales === 'string' ? [locales] : locales.concat();
                                for (i = 0; i < mod.langBundles.length; i += 1) {
                                    mods = [];
                                    loadDefaultBundle = false;
                                    name = mod.group + '-lang-' + mod.langBundles[i];
                                    for (j = 0; j < locales.length; j += 1) {
                                        m = this.getModule(name + '_' + locales[j].toLowerCase());
                                        if (m) {
                                            mods.push(m);
                                        } else {
                                            // if one of the requested locales is missing,
                                            // the default lang should be fetched
                                            loadDefaultBundle = true;
                                        }
                                    }
                                    if (!mods.length || loadDefaultBundle) {
                                        // falling back to the default lang bundle when needed
                                        m = this.getModule(name);
                                        if (m) {
                                            mods.push(m);
                                        }
                                    }
                                    // adding requirements for each lang bundle
                                    // (duplications are not a problem since they will be deduped)
                                    for (j = 0; j < mods.length; j += 1) {
                                        mod.langBundlesExpanded = mod.langBundlesExpanded.concat(this.getRequires(mods[j]), [mods[j].name]);
                                    }
                                }
                            }
                            return mod.langBundlesExpanded && mod.langBundlesExpanded.length ?
                                    [].concat(mod.langBundlesExpanded, r) : r;
                        };
                    }
            ];
        }
        for (var i = 0; i < YMedia.config.patches.length; i += 1) {YMedia.config.patches[i](YMedia, YMedia.Env._loader);}

                });

This Is the First Time I’ve Had Hope in 25 Years","link":"https://www.yahoo.com/news/am-school-shooting-survivor-first-164544881.html","summary":"Students are standing up to the gun lobby, the NRA and politicians","publisher":"Time","author":"devorah_heitner","propertyRegion":"YPROP:news","hosted":true,"publicationDate":"Tue, Feb 27 8:45 AM PST","comScoreMeta":"Yahoo - ABC News Network","leadItem":false,"body":{"incomplete_body":["<p>In December, 1992, I was 17 years old. I remember vividly the experience of hiding from an active shooter on campus at Simon’s Rock College in Great Barrington, Mass. It was the longest hour of my life. We hid in my friend’s bedroom, where a few of us had gathered to study for finals. We hunched down below the windows and barricaded the door and waited — angry and terrified. My friend, Galen Gibson, and our professor, Ñacuñán Saez, were murdered.</p>","<p>The shooter had enough ammunition to kill every one of the 300 students at our small liberal arts college, a haven for kids who needed an early exit from high school. Most of us were saved by his gun jamming.</p>","<p>But this is not about me. This is about <i>hope</i> — and maybe, finally, a chance for change.</p>","<p>By now you’ve heard of <a href=\"http://time.com/5168821/florida-school-shooting-gun-control/\" data-ylk=\"sec:giraffe_viewer;\">Emma Gonzalez</a>, a remarkable young woman who has helped <a href=\"http://time.com/5169436/florida-shooting-kids-gun-control-debate/\" data-ylk=\"sec:giraffe_viewer;\">light the spark of a movement</a> that I hope will deliver lasting change to how we prevent school shootings. A student of Marjory Stoneman Douglas High School in Parkland, Florida, she and her classmates are <a href=\"http://time.com/5169473/gun-control-florida-school-shooting/\" data-ylk=\"sec:giraffe_viewer;\">standing up</a> to the gun lobby, the NRA and the politicians who support them.</p>","<p>She led a crowd at a rally in the forceful incantation, <a href=\"https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=ZxD3o-9H1lY\" target=\"_blank\" data-ylk=\"sec:giraffe_viewer;\">“We call B.S.!”</a></p>","<p>A mixture of grief and anger in her voice, she somehow spoke with a clarity we haven’t seen on this issue. It felt like a turning point in U.S. history.</p>","<p>At least I hope it is.</p>","<h3>Where Inaction Leads</h3>","<p>After I survived the shooting, I withdrew into my trauma. Meanwhile, Gregory Gibson, the father of our murdered classmate, has <a href=\"https://www.npr.org/templates/transcript/transcript.php?storyId=570927239\" target=\"_blank\" data-ylk=\"sec:giraffe_viewer;\">worked tirelessly</a> alongside many others to create change. But I just wept at the grave of my friend and listened to other students in my dormitory cry themselves to sleep in the cold nights after the murders.</p>","<p>I am ashamed of my inaction for the past 25 years.</p>","<p>Sure, I was just a 17-year-old kid. Life was normal, and then suddenly it wasn’t. But every shooting makes me think of my incredible, beautiful, brilliant friend Galen.</p>","<p>My heart breaks again and again when I read about the traumatized survivors of mass shootings at <a href=\"http://time.com/4220590/dylan-klebold-mother-columbine-interview/\" data-ylk=\"sec:giraffe_viewer;\">Columbine</a> and <a href=\"http://time.com/4741270/virginia-tech-10-year-anniversary-guns/\" data-ylk=\"sec:giraffe_viewer;\">Virginia Tech</a> and <a href=\"http://www.washingtonpost.com/sf/national/2015/12/05/after-a-mass-shooting-a-survivors-life/\" target=\"_blank\" data-ylk=\"sec:giraffe_viewer;\">Umpqua</a> and <a href=\"http://time.com/5158804/marjory-stoneman-douglas-high-school-shooting/\" data-ylk=\"sec:giraffe_viewer;\">Stoneman Douglas</a>. When I see people <a href=\"http://www.modernhealthcare.com/article/20171227/NEWS/171229940\" target=\"_blank\" data-ylk=\"sec:giraffe_viewer;\">struggling to pay</a> for <a href=\"http://money.cnn.com/2017/10/25/pf/insurance/las-vegas-shooting-health-care/index.html\" target=\"_blank\" data-ylk=\"sec:giraffe_viewer;\">long-term care costs</a> and <a href=\"https://www.gofundme.com/anthonyborges\" target=\"_blank\" data-ylk=\"sec:giraffe_viewer;\">raising money to pay for their injuries and rehab</a>, I can’t believe we as a society are willing to accept these losses in the name of the Second Amendment. Our policies have so little empathy that mass shooting survivors, incapacitated by devastating injuries, can be left to fundraise for their own recovery. We guarantee the “protection” of guns, but not the protection of <a href=\"https://www.usnews.com/news/articles/2017-10-05/las-vegas-shooting-victims-facing-millions-of-dollars-in-medical-expenses\" target=\"_blank\" data-ylk=\"sec:giraffe_viewer;\">health care</a>.</p>"],"remaining_body":["<h3>Old Questions, New Energy</h3>","<p>People are starting to question why — not just on social media, but straight to the seats of power.</p>","<p>In a <a href=\"http://time.com/5169400/donald-trump-school-shooting-white-house-meeting/\" data-ylk=\"sec:giraffe_viewer;\">listening session</a> at the White House, Stoneman Douglas student Sam Zeif asked our President, “How is it <i>that</i> easy to buy this type of weapon? How did we not stop this after Columbine? After Sandy Hook?”</p>","<p>At a town hall later that evening broadcast by CNN, a student survivor from Stoneman Douglas, Cameron Kasky, <a href=\"http://time.com/5170065/florida-shooting-marco-rubio-gun-control/\" data-ylk=\"sec:giraffe_viewer;\">challenged</a> Florida Senator Marco Rubio to change: “Can you tell me right now that you will not accept a single donation from the NRA in the future?”</p>","<p>Emma, Sam, Cameron — they and the other survivors are now part of a club that no one wants to join. But when I watch these survivors come together, I feel hopeful.</p>","<h3>The Trauma Doesn’t Go Away</h3>","<p>I wish I could tell these young people that the trauma goes away. But I see how 25 years later, many of the friends I was with that night are still sad and traumatized again when each December rolls around — and with every milestone in our lives. Graduating. Starting a first job. Having a baby. At every step, you know that your friends were robbed of possibility.</p>","<p>The Simon’s Rock killer says that <a href=\"http://www.wcax.com/content/news/Vermonter-survivor-films-documentary-on-Simons-Rock-shooting-464246233.html\" target=\"_blank\" data-ylk=\"sec:giraffe_viewer;\">if he hadn’t been able to get a gun so easily</a>, he wouldn’t have been able to do what he did. If there is any chance that making it harder to get guns could have kept Galen Gibson and Ñacuñán Saez alive in 1992, how can we not fight for that? If it could have spared the survivors their physical injuries and emotional pain, how can we not speak up for that?</p>","<p>My son, who just turned nine, doesn’t know my story. Not yet. He was four when the <a href=\"http://time.com/5064957/nicole-hockley-sandy-hook/\" data-ylk=\"sec:giraffe_viewer;\">Sandy Hook massacre</a> happened, and all I wanted was for him <i>not</i> to be part of the the assembly where the kids at his Pre-K–8 school wrote cards for the people of Newtown. I couldn’t imagine that there was a “right” way to tell a 4-year-old about a “bad man” coming into a school and shooting children. The day after the <a href=\"http://time.com/5162936/florida-high-school-shooting-timeline/\" data-ylk=\"sec:giraffe_viewer;\">Parkland shooting</a>, a mother in Ohio got news that her child was in a school on lockdown. By her description <a href=\"https://www.facebook.com/leah.sjovold/posts/10159962381635557\" target=\"_blank\" data-ylk=\"sec:giraffe_viewer;\">in a Facebook post</a><b>,</b> she found herself on the floor, dizzy and disoriented. Reading her account gave me vertigo.</p>","<h3>A New Narrative from a New Generation</h3>","<p>To Emma Gonzalez, Sam Zeif, Cameron Kasky and the Stoneman Douglas students standing up with them:</p>","<p>Don’t listen when adults tell you something can’t change. Even though supposedly “nothing has changed” and it is still way too easy to get guns, a lot of other things have changed. One example: In the early ‘90s, when I attended Simon’s Rock, it seemed like everyone smoked. But 25 years later, I can’t remember the last time I’ve seen someone smoking a cigarette. Another example: My kid is confident and comfortable with using “they” as a pronoun for the people in his life who have non-binary genders. Change happens.</p>","<p>You are right to call B.S. on the idea that nothing can be done.</p>","<p>You have inspired me. As a mother, as an educator, as someone who is fundamentally optimistic about the ways young people can <i>create </i>change, I am excited to see what you will do.</p>","<p>You are part of a continuum of young activists that includes the <a href=\"http://time.com/4922121/dreamers-daca-undocumented-online/\" data-ylk=\"sec:giraffe_viewer;\">Dreamers</a> and the <a href=\"http://time.com/5171270/black-lives-matter-patrisse-cullors/\" data-ylk=\"sec:giraffe_viewer;\">Movement for Black Lives</a>. Your generation has the savvy and the tools and the motivation. Rise up. Fight back. Show up — whether it’s in Tallahassee, in D.C. or on social media. Channel your grief and frustration and rage into action. This is going to be a long struggle and the trauma of your losses may overwhelm you at times. Stay strong. Take care of each other. Love each other. We are listening. We are here with you.</p>"]},"property":"news","enable_lead":true,"cover_photo":{"img":{"src":"data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7","className":"Lead-s W-max","height":427,"width":640,"ratio":67,"thumb":"https://s2.yimg.com/lo/api/res/1.2/AeuBf3.upT5wgHW24AUZWQ--/YXBwaWQ9eW15O3c9MTY0O2g9MTY0O2ZpPWZpbGw7cHhvZmY9NTA7cHlvZmY9MDtzbT0x/http://media.zenfs.com/en-US/homerun/time_72/2c1dd77aeb6f8423d98d7b9fa4c21f47","lazySrc":"https://s3.yimg.com/lo/api/res/1.2/RHlJ0DelO0p_78XT9sjtkg--/YXBwaWQ9eW15O3E9NzU7dz02NDA7c209MQ--/http://media.zenfs.com/en-US/homerun/time_72/2c1dd77aeb6f8423d98d7b9fa4c21f47","lazyClass":"ImageLoader-Delayed"},"caption":null,"headline":null},"images":[],"count":0},{"type":"story","is_eligible":"false","id":"15eb1416-afab-34be-ac0c-ad92ba9e7d1d","categoryLabel":"Business","cluster_id":"0ce131c5-515e-3fe8-bfdb-301892a052bd","licensed":"true","title":"Gun company investors push for change after Florida school shooting","link":"https://www.yahoo.com/news/gun-company-investors-push-change-060002214.html","summary":"Socially responsible investors and asset management giant BlackRock plan to use their stakes to ask weapons manufacturers some hard questions A sign hangs on a fence at Marjory Stoneman Douglas high school in Parkland, Florida, following the mass shooting there earlier this month. Photograph: Rhona Wise/AFP/Getty Images","publisher":"The Guardian","author":"dominic_rushe_in_new_york","propertyRegion":"YPROP:news","embedded_images":[{"source":"http://media.zenfs.com/en-US/homerun/the_guardian_765/88dc4ae3befef94b451bb577f8c4b83a"},{"source":"http://media.zenfs.com/en-US/homerun/the_guardian_765/d45dd05a1cce21df664902e647a63340"},{"source":"https://ophan.theguardian.com/nojs/i.gif?platform=yahoo&url=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.theguardian.com%2Fus-news%2F2018%2Ffeb%2F28%2Fgun-company-investors-florida-school-shooting"}],"hosted":true,"publicationDate":"Tue, Feb 27 10:00 PM PST","comScoreMeta":"Yahoo - ABC News Network","leadItem":false,"body":{"incomplete_body":["<p>Socially responsible investors and asset management giant BlackRock plan to use their stakes to ask weapons manufacturers some hard questions</p>","<figure> \n <span class=\"Embed-Img D-b Ta-c\"><img src=\"data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7\" data-imageloader-src=\"https://s3.yimg.com/lo/api/res/1.2/SKBv_vVP.LDCjtNQXwIEAQ--/YXBwaWQ9eW15O3c9NjQwO3E9NzU7c209MQ--/http://media.zenfs.com/en-US/homerun/the_guardian_765/88dc4ae3befef94b451bb577f8c4b83a\" alt=\"A sign hangs on a fence at Marjory Stoneman Douglas high school in Parkland, Florida, following the mass shooting there earlier this month.\" width=\"640\" height=\"384\" class=\"Maw-100 ImageLoader-Delayed gu-image\" /></span> \n <figcaption> \n  <span class=\"element-image__caption\">A sign hangs on a fence at Marjory Stoneman Douglas high school in Parkland, Florida, following the mass shooting there earlier this month.</span> \n  <span class=\"element-image__credit\">Photograph: Rhona Wise/AFP/Getty Images</span> \n </figcaption> \n</figure>","<p>What if the answer to America’s guns crisis lies not with its government but with its gun companies? It’s a question that some investors are now asking and after the recent mass shooting in Florida, some see a path to change.</p>","<figure> \n <a href=\"https://interactive.guim.co.uk/embed/2017/11/break-the-cycle/embed.html\" data-ylk=\"sec:giraffe_viewer;\">left</a> \n</figure>","<p>While the deadly massacre at Marjory Stoneman Douglas high school in Parkland, Florida, this month sparked a national debate and made its survivors a powerful voice for a new generation of gun-control activists, there are no guarantees of meaningful change. America’s mass shootings can seem like a grim repetitive cycle of “thoughts and prayers” followed by political inaction, a brief pause, and then another mass shooting. </p>","<p>But this time, Judy Byron, coordinator of the Northwest Coalition for Responsible Investment at the Interfaith Center on Corporate Responsibility (ICCR) is hopeful something has changed.</p>","<p>“These high school kids are really changing the debate. I really see some hope this time,” she said. She aims to back their powerful rhetoric with money. </p>","<p>The ICCR is a coalition of 300 global institutional investors which control $400bn in managed assets for faith-based groups, academics, unions and others interested in socially responsible investment.</p>","<p>Normally, guns would not be on their list of good investments, but two years ago, outraged by the seemingly unending gun death toll in the US, the ICCR started encouraging its members to buy gun shares so that they would have a voice as shareholders. The campaign appears to be taking off.</p>"],"remaining_body":["<p>ICCR members have filed motions with the two largest listed US gun companies, Sturm Ruger and American Outdoor Brands (formerly Smith & Wesson) requesting reports detailing the companies’ efforts to make their products safer. It’s a move that could bring pressure to bear on gun companies to do more to make their products safer and harder to buy, even if Florida’s tragedy fails to move Washington to action.<br /></p>","<p>“We are not going to do away with guns but what are they [the gun companies] going to do to make them safer?” asked Byron. Technology allows us to lock up our phones when they are not in our possession, she said. “But if I left my gun out on the desk, you could use it. Why is that?” she said.</p>","<p>Until recently shareholder activists have tended to focus on “divestment” as their tactic to put pressure on gun companies. Many ethical funds refuse to hold shares in gun companies at all and following Florida’s shooting there have again been campaigns to press pension funds to drop their holdings.<br /></p>","<p>But those campaigns have been complicated in recent years by the rise of index funds – lower-cost funds that track the performance of various stock market indexes and hold shares in all their components. </p>","<p>BlackRock, the world’s largest asset manager with assets of $6tn, is a major player in index funds. As a result it owns significant chunks of gun companies Smith & Wesson and Sturm Ruger – not because it sees guns as a great investment but because they are constituents of major indexes like the Russell 2000 index for smaller companies.</p>","<p>Last week, BlackRock said it too intends to speak to weapons manufacturers and distributors “to understand their response” to the Florida high school shooting. It hasn’t yet said what it will do if it doesn’t like their replies but the company has form for effecting real change.</p>","<figure> \n <span class=\"Embed-Img D-b Ta-c\"><img src=\"data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7\" data-imageloader-src=\"https://s3.yimg.com/lo/api/res/1.2/_q3J17hQcOq1EEOzyDD3PQ--/YXBwaWQ9eW15O3c9NjQwO3E9NzU7c209MQ--/http://media.zenfs.com/en-US/homerun/the_guardian_765/d45dd05a1cce21df664902e647a63340\" alt=\"Larry Fink of BlackRock\" width=\"640\" height=\"384\" class=\"Maw-100 ImageLoader-Delayed gu-image\"></span> \n  <figcaption> \n   <span class=\"element-image__caption\">Larry Fink of BlackRock: ‘To prosper over time, every company must not only deliver financial performance, but also show how it makes a positive contribution to society.’</span> \n   <span class=\"element-image__credit\">Photograph: Bloomberg/Bloomberg via Getty Images</span> \n  </figcaption> </img>\n</figure>","<p>BlackRock’s founder, Larry Fink, <a href=\"https://www.nytimes.com/2018/01/15/business/dealbook/blackrock-laurence-fink-letter.html\" data-ylk=\"sec:giraffe_viewer;\">warned company executives in January</a> he expected them to behave as good citizens. “Society is demanding that companies, both public and private, serve a social purpose,” Fink wrote to CEOs. “To prosper over time, every company must not only deliver financial performance, but also show how it makes a positive contribution to society.”</p>","<p>The letter followed BlackRock’s decision last May to back a shareholder resolution to <a href=\"https://www.theguardian.com/business/2017/may/31/exxonmobil-climate-change-cost-shareholders\" data-ylk=\"sec:giraffe_viewer;\">force energy giant Exxon to be more open </a>about the impact of climate change on its business. </p>","<p>That resolution had long been championed by ICCR members including the pension funds of the Church of England but with BlackRock’s support it was passed by 62% of shareholders. “When we do not see progress despite ongoing engagement, or companies are insufficiently responsive to our efforts to protect the long-term economic interests of our clients, we will not hesitate to exercise our right to vote,” BlackRock said a <a href=\"https://www.blackrock.com/corporate/en-gb/literature/publication/blk-vote-bulletin-occidental-may-2017.pdf\" data-ylk=\"sec:giraffe_viewer;\">statement</a>.<br> </p>","<p>The Exxon victory could provide a model for change, said Byron. With BlackRock’s support, change is also possible at the gun companies, she said.</p>","<p>She also pointed to the success of campaigners against apartheid in South Africa who targeted companies investing in the country until it scrapped racial segregation.</p>","<p>“It took 20 years but it happened,” she said. “But this time we cannot take 20 years. I was a teacher and I just cannot imagine teaching in this environment.”</p>","<p>Adam Kanzer, managing director of corporate engagement at Domini Impact Investments, which manages socially responsible mutual funds, said BlackRock’s involvement was a significant early victory for the campaign,<br /></p>","<p>“They are going to take that meeting,” said Kanzer. “I am very, very pleased to see that big investors are starting to wake up.”<br /></p>","<p>He also said that pressure for change was likely to come from below. “If you manage a teachers’ pension fund, you have got to be hearing from your investors about this,” he said. “That feels like a real problem to me.”</p>","<p>But he worries that, as has so often been the case, attention spans are short and pressure for change could fizzle out. And that, in the end, America’s gun problem is an issue that needs “a public sector response. It is not going to be solved by the private sector alone.”</p>","<p>The first test will come in May when Sturm Ruger holds its annual shareholder meeting and shareholders will be asked to force the company to account for its “activities related to gun safety measures and the mitigation of harm associated with gun products”.</p>","<p>Even if they are not successful this time, the campaign will continue. “Something has to change,” said Byron.</p>","<figure> \n <a href=\"https://interactive.guim.co.uk/embed/2017/11/break-the-cycle/epic.html\" data-ylk=\"sec:giraffe_viewer;\">bottom</a>   <script type="text/javascript">
function _daTRK() {
    var daTrk = '-1';
    var daFr = 0;
    var cExpiry = 0;
        if (window.pageloadNonCollapsedAds && window.pageloadNonCollapsedAds.length > 0) {
        daTrk = '0';
        for (i=0; i<window.pageloadNonCollapsedAds.length; i++) {
            var daTRKDiv = document.getElementById("my-ads" + pageloadNonCollapsedAds[i]);
            if (daTRKDiv && daTRKDiv.offsetHeight === 0) {
                daTrk = '1';
                cExpiry = 10080;
                break;
            }
        }
    } else {
        var daTRKDiv = document.getElementById("my-adsFPAD");
        if (daTRKDiv ) {
            daTrk = '0';
            if (daTRKDiv.offsetHeight === 0) {
                cExpiry = 10080;
                    daTrk = '1';
                }
            }   
        }
    if (daFr || '1' === daTrk) {
        window.thamba = 1;
    }

    YUI().use('cookie', function(Y) {

        function fireThambaEvent() {
            Y.use('event', function(YM) {
                if(YM.Cookie.exists('thamba')) {
                    var clientSideVal = parseInt(YM.Cookie.get('thamba'), 10);
                    var serverSideVal = 0;
                    if(window.rapidPageConfig && 
                        window.rapidPageConfig.rapidConfig &&
                        window.rapidPageConfig.rapidConfig.keys &&
                        window.rapidPageConfig.rapidConfig.keys.abk) {
                        var value = window.rapidPageConfig.rapidConfig.keys.abk;

                        switch(value) {
                            case 'abp':
                                serverSideVal = 2;
                                break;
                            case 'other':
                                serverSideVal = 1;
                                break;
                        }
                    }

                    if(0 === serverSideVal && clientSideVal > serverSideVal) {
                        YM.Global.fire('thamba:value-change', {"clientVal": clientSideVal, "serverVal": serverSideVal});
                    }
                }
            });
        }

        var expires = new Date();
        expires.setMinutes(expires.getMinutes() + cExpiry);
        Y.Cookie.set('thamba', daTrk, {expires: expires, domain: location.hostname});
        if (typeof window.thamba != 'undefined') {
                    var DPba=new function(){this.detect=function(px,callback){var detected=false;var checksRemain=2;var error1=false;var error2=false;if(typeof callback!="function")return;px+="?ch=*&rn=*";function beforeCheck(callback,timeout){if(checksRemain==0|| timeout>1E3)callback(checksRemain==0&&detected);else setTimeout(function(){beforeCheck(callback,timeout*2)},timeout*2)}function checkImages(){if(--checksRemain)return;detected=!error1&&error2}var random=Math.random()*11;var img1=new Image;img1.onload=checkImages;img1.onerror=function(){error1=true;checkImages()};img1.src=px.replace(/\*/,1).replace(/\*/,random);var img2=new Image;img2.onload=checkImages;img2.onerror=function(){error2=true;checkImages()};img2.src=px.replace(/\*/,2).replace(/\*/,random);beforeCheck(callback,250)}}; 
        DPba.detect("/px.gif", function(usesABP) {
            if (usesABP) {
                var expires = new Date();
                expires.setMinutes(expires.getMinutes() + 10080);
                Y.Cookie.set('thamba', '2', {expires: expires, domain: location.hostname});
                fireThambaEvent();
            }
        });
        } else {
            fireThambaEvent();
        }
    });
}

        setTimeout(function() {window._daTRK(), 300});
